      </table> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/Trinidad_and_Tobago_national_basketball_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Trinidad and Tobago national basketball team">Trinidad and Tobago national basketball team</a>
      </div> 
      <p><a href="/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">Basketball</a> is commonly played in Trinidad and Tobago in colleges, universities and throughout various urban basketball courts. Its national team is one of the most successful teams in the Caribbean. At the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Basketball_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="Caribbean Basketball Championship">Caribbean Basketball Championship</a> it won four straight gold medals from 1986 to 1990. </p> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_sports">Other sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Trinidad_and_Tobago&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Other sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4> 
      <table class="box-Unreferenced_section plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation">
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <td class="mbox-image">
          <div style="width:52px">
           <a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399"></a>
          </div></td>
         <td class="mbox-text">
          <div class="mbox-text-span">
           This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Trinidad_and_Tobago&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Referencing_for_beginners" title="Help:Referencing for beginners">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span> <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">August 2019</span>)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small>
          </div></td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <p><a href="/wiki/Netball" title="Netball">Netball</a> has long been a popular sport in Trinidad and Tobago, although it has declined in popularity in recent years. At the <a href="/wiki/Netball_World_Championships" class="mw-redirect" title="Netball World Championships">Netball World Championships</a> they co-won the event in 1979, were runners up in 1987, and second runners up in 1983. </p>
      <p><a href="/wiki/Rugby_union_in_Trinidad_and_Tobago" title="Rugby union in Trinidad and Tobago">Rugby</a> is played in Trinidad and Tobago and continues to be a popular sport, and <a href="/wiki/Horse_racing" title="Horse racing">horse racing</a> is regularly followed in the country. </p>
      <p>There is also the <a href="/wiki/Trinidad_and_Tobago_national_baseball_team" title="Trinidad and Tobago national baseball team">Trinidad and Tobago national baseball team</a> which is controlled by the Baseball/Softball Association of Trinidad and Tobago, and represents the nation in international competitions. The team is a provisional member of the <a href="/wiki/Pan_American_Baseball_Confederation" class="mw-redirect" title="Pan American Baseball Confederation">Pan American Baseball Confederation</a>. </p>
      <p>There are a number of 9 and 18-hole <a href="/wiki/Golf" title="Golf">golf</a> courses on Trinidad and Tobago. The most established is the St Andrews Golf Club, Maraval in Trinidad (commonly referred to as Moka), and there is a newer course at Trincity, near Piarco Airport called Millennium Lakes. There are 18-hole courses at Chaguramas and Point-a-Pierre and nine-hole courses at Couva and St Madeline. Tobago has two 18-hole courses. The older of the two is at Mount Irvine, with the Magdalena Hotel &amp; Golf Club (formerly Tobago Plantations) being built more recently. </p>
      <p>Although a minor sport, bodybuilding is of growing interest in Trinidad and Tobago. <a href="/wiki/Darrem_Charles" title="Darrem Charles">Darrem Charles</a>, a former world class body builder, is from Trinidad and Tobago. </p>
      <p>Dragonboat is also another water-sport that has been rapidly growing over the years. Introduced in 2006. the fraternity made consistent strides in having more members a part of the TTDBF (Trinidad and Tobago Dragonboat Federation) as well as performing on an international level such as the 10th IDBF World Nations Dragon Boat Championships in Tampa, Florida in the US in 2011. </p>
      <p><a href="/wiki/Claude_Noel_(boxer)" title="Claude Noel (boxer)">Claude Noel</a> is a former world champion in professional boxing. He was born in Tobago. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="National_symbols">National symbols</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Trinidad_and_Tobago&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: National symbols">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/National_symbols_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago" title="National symbols of Trinidad and Tobago">National symbols of Trinidad and Tobago</a>
      </div> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Flag">Flag</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Trinidad_and_Tobago&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Flag">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago" title="Flag of Trinidad and Tobago">Flag of Trinidad and Tobago</a>
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Flag_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg/220px-Flag_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="132" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Flag_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg/330px-Flag_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Flag_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg/440px-Flag_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="480"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>The flag of Trinidad and Tobago
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>The flag was chosen by the Independence committee in 1962. Red, black and white symbolise the warmth of the people, the richness of the earth and water respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-gov_192-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gov-192">[188]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">[189]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Coat_of_arms">Coat of arms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Trinidad_and_Tobago&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Coat of arms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago" title="Coat of arms of Trinidad and Tobago">Coat of arms of Trinidad and Tobago</a>
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Coat_of_arms_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Coat_of_arms_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg/220px-Coat_of_arms_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="204" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Coat_of_arms_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg/330px-Coat_of_arms_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Coat_of_arms_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg/440px-Coat_of_arms_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="770" data-file-height="713"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Coat_of_Arms_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>The coat of arms of Trinidad and Tobago
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>The coat of arms was designed by the Independence committee, and features the <a href="/wiki/Scarlet_ibis" title="Scarlet ibis">scarlet ibis</a> (native to Trinidad), the <a href="/wiki/Rufous-vented_chachalaca" title="Rufous-vented chachalaca">cocrico</a> (native to Tobago) and hummingbird. The shield bears three ships, representing both the Trinity, and the three ships that Columbus sailed.<sup id="cite_ref-gov_192-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gov-192">[188]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Orders_and_decorations">Orders and decorations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Trinidad_and_Tobago&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Orders and decorations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>There are five categories and thirteen classes of national awards:<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">[190]</a></sup> </p> 
      <ul>
       <li>The <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Republic_of_Trinidad_and_Tobago" title="Order of the Republic of Trinidad and Tobago">Order of the Republic of Trinidad and Tobago</a> (formerly The <a href="/wiki/Trinity_Cross" title="Trinity Cross">Trinity Cross</a> Medal of the Order of the Trinity) in Gold only</li> 
       <li>The <a href="/wiki/Chaconia_Medal" title="Chaconia Medal">Chaconia Medal</a>, in Gold, Silver and Bronze</li> 
       <li>The <a href="/wiki/Hummingbird_Medal" title="Hummingbird Medal">Hummingbird Medal</a>, in Gold, Silver and Bronze</li> 
       <li>The Public Service Medal of Merit, in Gold, Silver and Bronze</li> 
       <li>The Medal for the Development of Women, in Gold, Silver and Bronze</li>
      </ul> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="National_anthem_and_national_songs">National anthem and national songs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Trinidad_and_Tobago&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: National anthem and national songs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Forged_from_the_Love_of_Liberty" title="Forged from the Love of Liberty">Forged from the Love of Liberty</a>
      </div> 
      <p>The national anthem of the twin-island state is "<a href="/wiki/Forged_from_the_Love_of_Liberty" title="Forged from the Love of Liberty">Forged from the Love of Liberty</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">[191]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">[192]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Other national songs include "God Bless Our Nation"<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">[193]</a></sup> and "Our Nation's Dawning".<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">[194]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="National_flower">National flower</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Trinidad_and_Tobago&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: National flower">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Warszewiczia_coccinea" title="Warszewiczia coccinea">Warszewiczia coccinea</a>
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Chaconia_UWI_2005b.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Chaconia_UWI_2005b.jpg/220px-Chaconia_UWI_2005b.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Chaconia_UWI_2005b.jpg/330px-Chaconia_UWI_2005b.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Chaconia_UWI_2005b.jpg/440px-Chaconia_UWI_2005b.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="768"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Chaconia_UWI_2005b.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>The Chaconia (<i><a href="/wiki/Warszewiczia_coccinea" title="Warszewiczia coccinea">Warszewiczia coccinea</a></i>) is the national flower of Trinidad and Tobago
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>The national flower of Trinidad and Tobago is the <a href="/wiki/Warszewiczia_coccinea" title="Warszewiczia coccinea">chaconia</a> flower. It was chosen as the national flower because it is an indigenous flower that has witnessed the history of Trinidad and Tobago. It was also chosen as the national flower because of its red colour that resembles the red of the national flag and coat of arms and because it blooms around the Independence Day of Trinidad and Tobago.<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">[195]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="National_birds">National birds</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Trinidad_and_Tobago&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: National birds">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Scarlet_ibis" title="Scarlet ibis">Scarlet ibis</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rufous-vented_chachalaca" title="Rufous-vented chachalaca">Rufous-vented chachalaca</a>
      </div> 
      <p>The national birds of Trinidad and Tobago are the <a href="/wiki/Scarlet_ibis" title="Scarlet ibis">scarlet ibis</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Rufous-vented_chachalaca" title="Rufous-vented chachalaca">cocrico</a>. The scarlet ibis is kept safe by the government by living in the Caroni Bird Sanctuary which was set up by the government for the protection of these birds. The Cocrico is more indigenous to the island of Tobago and are more likely to be seen in the forest.<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">[196]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Hummingbird" title="Hummingbird">hummingbird</a> is considered another symbol of Trinidad and Tobago due to its significance to the indigenous peoples, however, it is not a national bird.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">[197]</a></sup> </p> 
      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional"> 
       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 235px">
        <div style="width: 235px"> 
         <div class="thumb" style="width: 230px;">
          <div style="margin:23.5px auto;">
           <a href="/wiki/File:Scarlet_Ibises_(5535961926).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Scarlet_Ibises_%285535961926%29.jpg/200px-Scarlet_Ibises_%285535961926%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="143" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Scarlet_Ibises_%285535961926%29.jpg/300px-Scarlet_Ibises_%285535961926%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Scarlet_Ibises_%285535961926%29.jpg/400px-Scarlet_Ibises_%285535961926%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3945" data-file-height="2817"></a>
          </div>
         </div> 
         <div class="gallerytext"> 
          <p>The scarlet ibis birds flying over the <a href="/wiki/Caroni_Swamp" title="Caroni Swamp">Caroni Swamp</a> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div></li> 
       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 235px">
        <div style="width: 235px"> 
         <div class="thumb" style="width: 230px;">
          <div style="margin:15.5px auto;">
           <a href="/wiki/File:Rvchachalaca102.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Rvchachalaca102.JPG/200px-Rvchachalaca102.JPG" decoding="async" width="200" height="159" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Rvchachalaca102.JPG/300px-Rvchachalaca102.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Rvchachalaca102.JPG/400px-Rvchachalaca102.JPG 2x" data-file-width="408" data-file-height="324"></a>
          </div>

         <tr>
          <td class="navbox-abovebelow" colspan="2">
           <div>
            <b>N.B.:</b> Territories in <i>italics</i> are parts of transregional sovereign states or non-sovereign dependencies. 
            <p><sup>^</sup> These three <a href="/wiki/Dutch_Caribbean" title="Dutch Caribbean">Dutch Caribbean</a> territories form the <a href="/wiki/SSS_islands" title="SSS islands">SSS islands</a>. </p>
            <p><sup>*</sup> These three <a href="/wiki/Dutch_Caribbean" title="Dutch Caribbean">Dutch Caribbean</a> territories form the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Netherlands" title="Caribbean Netherlands">BES islands</a>. </p>
            <p><sup>†</sup> <a href="/wiki/Physical_geography" title="Physical geography">Physiographically</a>, these are <a href="/wiki/Island#Continental_islands" title="Island">continental islands</a> not a part of the volcanic Windward Islands arc. However, based on proximity, these islands are sometimes grouped with the <a href="/wiki/Windward_Islands" title="Windward Islands">Windward Islands</a> culturally and politically. </p>
            <p><sup>~</sup> <a href="/wiki/Territorial_dispute" title="Territorial dispute">Disputed territories</a> administered by <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a>. </p>
            <p><sup>#</sup> Physiographically, <a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">Bermuda</a> is an isolated <a href="/wiki/Island#Oceanic_islands" title="Island">oceanic island</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">North Atlantic Ocean</a>, not a part of the Antilles, West Indies, Caribbean, North American continental mainland or South American continental mainland. Usually grouped with Northern American countries based on proximity; occasionally grouped with the Caribbean region culturally. </p> <sup>ǂ</sup> <a href="/wiki/Territorial_dispute" title="Territorial dispute">Disputed territories</a> administered by <a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">Guyana</a>.
           </div></td>
         </tr>
